It manages the entire module resolution and loading pipeline through several key methods:\\n\\n- `getModuleJobForImport()`: Gets or creates a ModuleJob for dynamic imports\\n- `resolve()`: Delegates to customized resolve hooks or calls `defaultResolve`\\n- `load()`: Delegates to customized load hooks or calls `defaultLoad`\\n- `loadAndTranslate()`: Loads source and translates it into a ModuleWrap\\n- `importSyncForRequire()`: Handles synchronous ESM loading from CommonJS require()\\n\\nThe ModuleLoader can be customized with user-provided hooks through the `CustomizedModuleLoader` class, which delegates to a **HooksProxy** (lib/internal/modules/esm/hooks.js) that manages loader hooks in a worker thread.\\n\\n## Module Resolution\\n\\nThe **defaultResolve** function (lib/internal/modules/esm/resolve.js:1011) performs module specifier resolution. It supports:\\n\\n- Relative path resolution\\n- Package.json exports/imports field resolution via `packageExportsResolve`\\n- Conditional exports based on environment conditions\\n- Built-in module detection (node: protocol)\\n- File protocol handling\\n- Data URLs\\n\\nFor CJS-ESM interop, the **finalizeEsmResolution** function (lib/internal/modules/cjs/loader.js:1258) validates and finalizes ESM resolution in the CommonJS loader context, checking for encoded path separators and verifying the module exists.\\n\\n## Module Loading and Translation\\n\\nThe **defaultLoad** function (lib/internal/modules/esm/load.js) loads module source code from various protocols:\\n\\n- **file:** protocol: Read from filesystem\\n- **data:** protocol: Parse data URLs\\n- **node:** protocol: Use built-in module code\\n\\nThe **translators** (lib/internal/modules/esm/translators.js:81) map handles different module formats:\\n\\n- 'module': Standard ES modules (JavaScript source)\\n- 'commonjs': CommonJS modules (wrapped for ESM)\\n- 'json': JSON files\\n- 'wasm': WebAssembly modules\\n- Other formats for TypeScript and custom types\\n\\nFormat detection is handled by **defaultGetFormat** (lib/internal/modules/esm/get_format.js:240), which uses:\\n\\n- File extensions from **extensionFormatMap** (lib/internal/modules/esm/formats.js:14)\\n- MIME types via **mimeToFormat** (lib/internal/modules/esm/formats.js:36)\\n- Package.json type fields\\n- File content analysis (detect module vs commonjs syntax)\\n\\n## Module Compilation and ModuleJob Pipeline\\n\\nThe **compileSourceTextModule** function (lib/internal/modules/esm/utils.js:336) bridges JavaScript and C++ to compile source into a ModuleWrap. It calls the native **ModuleWrap::CompileSourceTextModule** (src/module_wrap.cc:337, src/module_wrap.h:81), which:\\n\\n- Compiles JavaScript/WebAssembly source using V8's compiler\\n- Creates a v8::Module object\\n- Wraps it in a ModuleWrap C++ object\\n- Sets up host-defined options for proper module behavior\\n- Optionally uses code caching\\n\\nThe **ModuleJob** class (lib/internal/modules/esm/module_job.js:72) wraps a compiled ModuleWrap and handles:\\n\\n- **_link()**: Resolves and links all module dependencies recursively\\n- **_instantiate()**: Instantiates the module and its dependency graph\\n- **run()**: Evaluates the module asynchronously\\n\\nThe **ModuleJobSync** class (lib/internal/modules/esm/module_job.js:310) provides synchronous variants for require() of ESM in imported CommonJS modules.\\n\\n## Caching Infrastructure\\n\\nThe **ResolveCache** (lib/internal/modules/esm/module_map.js:25) caches module resolution results by specifier and import attributes, ensuring consistent resolution per the ECMAScript specification.\\n\\nThe **LoadCache** (lib/internal/modules/esm/module_map.js) caches compiled ModuleWrap objects to avoid recompilation.\\n\\n## Entry Point Detection\\n\\nThe **shouldUseESMLoader** function (lib/internal/modules/run_main.js:64) determines whether the main entry point should be loaded as an ES module based on:\\n\\n- .mjs file extension\\n- --experimental-default-type flag\\n- package.json type field\\n- Experimental loader presence\\n- File existence checks\\n\\n## Import Metadata and Assertions\\n\\nThe **initializeImportMeta** function (lib/internal/modules/esm/initialize_import_meta.js:56) sets up the import.meta object with:\\n\\n- url: The module's URL\\n- dirname/filename: File path information\\n- resolve: Dynamic resolution function\\n\\nThe **validateAttributes** function (lib/internal/modules/esm/assert.js:55) enforces import assertions (e.g., `import json from 'data.json' with { type: 'json' }`).\\n\\n## Native Binding\\n\\nThe **ModuleWrap** C++ class (src/module_wrap.h:36, src/module_wrap.cc:53) serves as the low-level interface between JavaScript and V8's module system:\\n\\n- Stores v8::Module references\\n- Provides instantiation and evaluation methods\\n- Manages module internal fields (URL, context, synthetic evaluation steps)\\n- Implements weak references and garbage collection integration\\n\\n## Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n- **fetch_module.js**: Handles HTTP/HTTPS module fetching with caching\\n- **create_dynamic_module.js**: import attributes, ensuring consistent resolution per the ECMAScript specification.\\n\\nThe **LoadCache** (lib/internal/modules/esm/module_map.js) caches compiled ModuleWrap objects to avoid File path information\\n- resolve: Dynamic resolution function\\n\\nThe **validateAttributes** function (lib/internal/modules/esm/assert.js:55) enforces import assertions (e.g., `import json from 'data.json' with { type: 'json' }`).\\n\\n## Native Binding\\n\\nThe **ModuleWrap** C++ class (src/module_wrap.h:36, src/module_wrap.cc:53) serves as the low-level interface between JavaScript and V8's module system:\\n\\n- Stores v8::Module references\\n- Provides instantiation and evaluation methods\\n- Manages module internal fields (URL, context, synthetic evaluation steps)\\n- Implements
